[30;1m501 | [0m[35mwill be initialized at module load time, Confuse provides a `LazyConfig`[0m
[30;1m502 | [0m[35mobject that loads your configuration files on demand instead of when the[0m
[30;1m503 | [0m[35mobject is constructed. (Doing complicated stuff like parsing YAML at[0m
[30;1m504 | [0m[35mmodule load time is generally considered a Bad Idea.)[0m
